< Review>
Came here to look around and ask about booth pricing since I buy/sell vintage. The last time I was here was a few years ago. I've bought furniture, clothes, and even traded here before. Stopped coming because I got busy with work/marriage/mom life. Upon entering, the air conditioner felt really nice! That makes shopping more enjoyable but the horrible customer service today made me leave asap. First of all, this girl made no effort to talk to me, ask me what I was looking for, or even carry my items to the fitting room because I was obviously carrying a baby. I tried to make small talk and she said nothing back, maybe just an "oh". I was finished trying on, didn't see her, so I just left them on the counter. She said nothing and just put them back (I assume). What if I wanted to buy them? I left quickly, said, "bye thank you" and got, "have a nice day" okay yeah whatever. I would never sell anything here with service like that. I was the ONLY person in the store the whole time. I got in my car and she was snapping photos of items probably to post online... yet makes zero effort to make a sale right under her nose. Lame. Why would I even come back? I've bought things off of craigslist and received better service. One star for air conditioning...< /Review>

< review>
I've had the privilege of working for Rancho and its facilities for several months now and it has been a pleasure helping manage the pool and its staff members. Through careful attentiveness to members and their needs, this staff (especially the aquatics staff) go above and beyond what many "swim-&-gyms" require with their customer engagement.

< Review>
Customer service was quite good, really . I was attended to in short order even though the person ahead of me seemed a bit indecisive and was taking longer than usual.
Another employee, the manager I believe, took my order while the other customer completed his order with the other service order taker.
I had the 12"  tuna sub on honey wheat. It was a pretty good sandwich, a nice change for me from the usual lunch meats. The sub was freshly prepared, with my choice of flavorful nutritious veggies as I watched it being made. I chose american cheese, (not a vegetable, I know),  a few tomato slices and spinach leaves with some green bell peppers. It was both hearty and good tasting.</Review>

<Time>1505434590900< /Time>< Review>
I frequently wonder how Stater Bros. can justify the prices for their produce. It always looks like it's gone 10 rounds with Mike Tyson and had to be put in a medically induced coma to recover. Their prices on most non-food items are on par with most grocery stores, which is about + $1-3 more than you would pay at Target or Walmart. Their selection is limited for most food items, which means a few big name brands and then their own brand. If you just need basic items, Stater Bros. will have something- it might not be the quality you're used to, but it will probably have the item. Their meat selection is very limited compared to other grocery stores. If you're shopping for meat, shop elsewhere. Same with bakery and deli items, most Stater Bros. don't have a dedicated counter for them to be ordered from, just a cold case or a few shelves.

So, if you have an option, go to a different grocery store. If you don't, you'll probably find some form of what you're looking for at Stater Bros.< /Review>
